    SELECT "e"."Id", "e"."BatchId", "e"."CorrelationId", "e"."CreatedAt", "e"."DataFim", "e"."DataInicio", "e"."Entidade", "e"."LatenciaMediaMs", "e"."MensagemErro", "e"."PaginaAtual", "e"."StackTrace", "e"."Status", "e"."ThroughputRegistrosPorSegundo", "e"."TipoExecucao", "e"."TotalPaginas", "e"."TotalRegistrosAtualizados", "e"."TotalRegistrosComErro", "e"."TotalRegistrosInseridos", "e"."TotalRegistrosLidos", "e"."TotalRegistrosProcessados", "e"."UpdatedAt"
    FROM "ETLBatches" AS "e"
    WHERE "e"."Id" = @__loteId_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS "e1"
LEFT JOIN "ETLBatchItems" AS "e0" ON "e1"."Id" = "e0"."ETLBatchId"
ORDER BY "e1"."Id"
